<TagTitle slot="title">

# Client Announcements Endpoints

</TagTitle>

</Tag>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/createannouncement [#operation-createannouncement]

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create Announcement_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a textual announcement visible to some set of users based on department and location.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationRequestBodySection slot="request-body">

<Section>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Request Body [#operation-createannouncement_request]

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content">

<OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection slot="request-body-description">

Announcement content

</OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection>

<ExpandableSection>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="audienceFilters"
  headingId="operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters"
  typeInfo={{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter\">FacetFilter</a>","children":[{"label":"FacetFilter","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter\">FacetFilter</a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters [#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableBreakout
  slot="entry"
  id="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"

  parentId="audienceFilters"
  hasFrontMatter={false}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandableBreakoutTitle slot="title">

#### FacetFilter [#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter]

</ExpandableBreakoutTitle>

<ExpandableBreakoutDescription slot="description">

</ExpandableBreakoutDescription>

<ExpandableBreakoutExamples slot="examples">

</ExpandableBreakoutExamples>

<ExpandableBreakoutDefaultValue slot="defaultValue">

</ExpandableBreakoutDefaultValue>

</ExpandableBreakout>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_fieldName"
  headingId="operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter_fieldname"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### fieldName [#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter_fieldname]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
owner
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_groupName"
  headingId="operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter_groupname"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName [#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter_groupname]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_values"
  headingId="operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter_values"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter_values_facetfiltervalue\">FacetFilterValue</a>","children":[{"label":"FacetFilterValue","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter_values_facetfiltervalue\">FacetFilterValue</a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values [#operation-createannouncement_request_audiencefilters_facetfilter_values]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandableProperty

  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### postType [#operation-createannouncement_request_posttype]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

This determines whether this is an external-link post or a regular announcement post. TEXT - Regular announcement that can contain rich text. LINK - Announcement that is linked to an external site.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName [#operation-createannouncement_responses_200_application-json_audiencefilters_facetfilter_groupname]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

##### values [#operation-createannouncement_responses_200_application-json_audiencefilters_facetfilter_values]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions [#operation-createannouncement_responses_200_application-json_author_metadata_permissions]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

##### permissions [#operation-createannouncement_responses_200_application-json_updatedby_metadata_permissions]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/updateannouncement [#operation-updateannouncement]

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update Announcement_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Update a textual announcement visible to some set of users based on department and location.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationRequestBodySection slot="request-body">

<Section>

### Request Body [#operation-updateannouncement_request]

</SectionTitle>

Announcement content. Id need to be specified for the announcement.

##### audienceFilters [#operation-updateannouncement_request_audiencefilters]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

```

```

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions [#operation-updateannouncement_responses_200_application-json_author_metadata_permissions]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions [#operation-updateannouncement_responses_200_application-json_updatedby_metadata_permissions]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>
